### [282] [When Mobile Crowdsourcing Meets Queueing Systems: Human-in-the-Loop Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18392)
*Hongbo Li,Lingjie Duan,Ness B. Shroff*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文研究服务系统中顾客利用拥塞信息选择队列时，个体激励与系统学习之间的权衡。自私顾客过度探索导致无限价格无政府状态（PoA），作者设计了动态侧支付机制，保证PoA低于2，并通过真实数据集验证了有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在服务系统中（如餐厅、主题公园、路网），顾客依赖众包平台获取实时拥塞信息做决策。但拥塞报告会过时，系统需要持续探索状态不确定的服务台。然而自私顾客为避免降低自身服务效用，不愿承担探索成本，导致个体激励与系统学习之间存在根本性矛盾。

Method: 1) 理论分析：证明短视服务器选择可导致无限PoA，单服务器场景下PoA下界随缓冲区增大而减小，多服务器场景下PoA上界随服务器数增加而减小。2) 机制设计：提出动态侧支付机制，周期性地对部分顾客收费并对其他顾客奖励，抑制过度探索，同时保持事后预算平衡。3) 实证验证：使用真实数据集进行实验。

Result: 1) 短视选择可导致无限大的效率损失（无限PoA）。2) 现有非货币信息机制无法解决该问题。3) 提出的动态侧支付机制将PoA控制在2以下。4) 真实数据集实验表明该机制在平均情况也表现良好。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了拥塞信息环境下顾客自利行为与系统学习之间的冲突，并证明通过精心设计的动态侧支付机制可以协调二者，在保证预算平衡的同时将效率损失控制在常数范围内。

Abstract: In service systems, customers now rely on congestion information before deciding which queue or server to join, from restaurants and theme-park attractions to road networks. We study this setting as human-in-the-loop learning (HILL), where customers both consume and generate time-sensitive congestion information through crowdsourcing platforms. Because congestion reports become stale, efficient system operation requires continued exploration of servers whose current states are uncertain. Yet selfish customers avoid such exploration when it reduces their immediate service utility, even though their observations would benefit future customers. We analyze this tension between individual incentives and system-wide learning in queueing systems with endogenous congestion. We first show that myopic server choices can induce an infinite price of anarchy (PoA): decentralized customers may cause arbitrarily large efficiency losses by overexploring servers that are likely congested. In the single-server case, we prove that the lower bound on PoA decreases as buffer size grows, while in the multi-server case the upper bound decreases as the number of servers increases. We further show that existing informational, non-monetary mechanisms for exploration-exploitation with exogenous information fail in our setting, as customers' choices directly reshape the queue states and still lead to infinite PoA. To address this challenge, we design a dynamic side-payment mechanism that periodically charges some customers and rewards others, discouraging excessive exploration while maintaining ex-post budget balance. The mechanism coordinates congestion management and information acquisition across heterogeneous servers, and guarantees PoA below 2. Beyond worst-case analysis, experiments using real datasets demonstrate that the proposed mechanism also achieves strong average-case performance.

### [284] [EFX Allocations Exist on Multi-Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18665)
*Mahyar Afshinmehr,Arash Ashuri,Pouria Mahmoudkhan,Kurt Mehlhorn,Amir Mohammad Shahrezaei*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文解决了多图估值下EFX分配存在性的开放问题，证明在可取消估值（加法估值的严格超类）下EFX分配总是存在，并给出了多项式时间算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: EFX分配的存在性是公平分配领域的核心开放问题。此前仅在简单图（每对代理至多一个共同价值物品）中证明EFX存在，而多图（允许多个物品被同一对代理共同估值）情形仅有部分近似结果。本文旨在彻底解决多图下的EFX存在性问题。

Method: 作者将图限制从简单图推广到多图，并将估值函数从加法推广到可取消估值（加法估值的严格超类）。构造了多项式时间算法来证明EFX分配的存在性。

Result: 成功证明在多图实例且代理具有可取消估值函数时，EFX分配总是存在，并且可以在多项式时间内计算出这样的分配。

Conclusion: 本文为EFX存在性结果增添了新的重要一笔，是少数适用于任意数量代理的EFX存在性结论之一，推动了公平分配领域核心开放问题的解决。

Abstract: We study the fair allocation of indivisible goods among agents, with a focus on limiting envy. A central fairness notion is envy-freeness up to any good (EFX), which requires that any envy toward another agent vanishes after the removal of any single good from the latter's bundle. The existence of EFX allocations is considered a major open problem in fair division. So far, it has only been established in limited settings.
  Christodoulou et al. [2023] proved the existence of EFX allocations for graphical valuations. In this setting, the agents correspond to the nodes of an underlying graph, and the goods correspond to the edges, and any good has positive value only for the endpoints of the corresponding edge. Their proof crucially relies on the restriction that the graph is simple, meaning that for any pair of agents, there is at most one good that has value to both.
  For multigraph valuations, where multiple goods may be valued by the same pair of agents, only partial results are known. Amanatidis et al. [2024] and Kaviani et al. [2025] obtained 2/3 and sqrt(2)/2 approximations of EFX, respectively; Kaviani et al. [2024] established existence under restricted additive valuations; and Afshinmehr et al. [2025a] proved existence under the assumption that the shortest cycle containing non-parallel edges has length at least 4.
  In this paper, we resolve this open problem by proving the existence of EFX allocations for multigraph instances under cancelable valuations, a strict superclass of additive valuation functions. Our proof is algorithmic and computes such allocations in polynomial time when the valuation functions are cancelable. This work contributes to the small number of EFX existence results that apply to an arbitrary number of agents.

</details>


### [285] [Epistemic Pairwise Maximin Share](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18921)
*Michal Feldman,Amos Fiat,Yael Nissan,Tomasz Ponitka*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的公平分配概念——认知成对最大最小份额（EPMMS），是PMMS的认知松弛版本。主要结果表明：(1) 对于加性估值，存在4/5-EPMMS分配并可高效计算；(2) 对于双值估值，EPMMS分配存在并可高效计算，甚至能得到更强的EGMMS保证；(3) 在MMS分配可能不存在的两种场景（三个加性智能体或两类加性智能体）中，EPMMS分配仍然存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: PMMS比EFX更强，但人们对PMMS的了解远少于EFX。近期研究表明从认知视角松弛EFX能取得显著进展，这自然引发了一个问题：类似方法能否推进对PMMS的理解？本文正是基于这一动机，首次研究PMMS的认知松弛版本EPMMS。

Method: 本文采用认知松弛（epistemic relaxation）的方法，将PMMS放松为EPMMS。针对不同估值类型（加性、双值）分别设计算法，并通过理论分析证明EPMMS分配的存在性与计算有效性。特别地，对于双值估值，进一步实现了更强的认知群体最大最小份额（EGMMS）。

Result: (1) 加性估值下，4/5-EPMMS分配存在且可高效计算；(2) 双值估值下，EPMMS（甚至EGMMS）分配存在且可高效计算；(3) 在三个加性智能体或两类加性智能体的场景中，即使MMS可能不存在，EPMMS分配仍然存在。

Conclusion: EPMMS作为PMMS的认知松弛，在多个设定下优于MMS的可行性，为公平分配问题提供了新的理论保证。这项工作填补了PMMS研究的空白，并展示了认知视角在公平分配领域的强大推广能力。

Abstract: We introduce epistemic pairwise maximin share (EPMMS), a new fairness notion for fair division of indivisible goods. Two fundamental notions in this setting are envy-freeness up to any item (EFX) and pairwise maximin share (PMMS), with PMMS being stronger than EFX. While EFX has been extensively studied, far less is known about PMMS. Recent work shows that relaxing EFX via an epistemic perspective leads to substantial progress on the EFX problem, raising the question of whether a similar approach can advance our understanding of PMMS. Motivated by this, we initiate the study of EPMMS, the epistemic relaxation of PMMS. EPMMS is more challenging than EEFX: the key approaches underlying recent progress on epistemic EFX inherently fail to extend to EPMMS.
  We establish the following results. (1) For additive valuations, $4/5$-EPMMS allocations exist and can be efficiently computed. (2) For bivalued valuations, EPMMS allocations exist and can be efficiently computed; in fact, we obtain the stronger guarantee of epistemic groupwise maximin share (EGMMS), which also strengthens the existence of MMS allocations for this setting. (3) We prove that EPMMS allocations exist in two settings where MMS allocations need not exist: instances with three additive agents or two types of additive agents.

</details>


### [286] [Convergence of Replicator Dynamics in the Repeated Prisoner's Dilemma with Restarts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18965)
*Benedict Russell,Chin-wing Leung,Paolo Turrini*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文研究在触发重启机制下的重复囚徒困境博弈，发现增加策略长度能促进合作涌现，且稳定策略需要包含初始背叛的"考验期"。尽管存在最优合作序列，智能体更偏好具有更长考验期的次优序列，因其具有更大的吸引域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在触发重启机制下，自私智能体在重复囚徒困境中面临合作与剥削的张力，作者旨在探究合作行为如何在这种机制下涌现并保持稳定。

Method: 将问题建模为参数化标准型博弈，智能体采用长度为m的策略序列。通过复制动力学分析混合种群中的收敛行为，推导稳定策略的精确计数公式，并分析参数条件。

Result: 增加策略长度促进合作涌现与稳定；给出了受限策略长度的精确收敛保证；推导了稳定序列的精确计数公式；发现稳定策略必须包含初始背叛（"考验期"）然后无限合作。

Conclusion: 虽然存在最优合作序列，但智能体倾向于选择具有更长考验期的次优序列，因为这些序列拥有更大的吸引域，即从进化动力学角度更具优势。

Abstract: We investigate a population of self-interested agents playing a repeated Prisoner's Dilemma under the trigger-restart mechanism. Under such a mechanism, agents play a sequence of symmetric games with their partner, and restart the interaction if their actions disagree. Our work focuses on the convergence of replicator dynamics in a well-mixed population of agents, where the emergence of cooperation is challenged by the individual incentive for exploitation. Formulating the corresponding parametrised normal-form game, with agents each adopting a length-m strategy sequence, we show that increasing the strategy length enables cooperation to emerge and stabilise. We provide exact convergence guarantees for restricted strategy lengths and, in the general payoff configuration, provide the necessary parametric conditions for the stability of cooperative strategies. By deriving an exact formula for the number of stable sequences, we find structural properties necessary for stability, as agents must learn to initially defect - the so-called "hazing period" - before cooperating indefinitely. Our analysis shows that, while optimal cooperative sequences exist, agents favour less-optimal sequences with a longer hazing period, which possess larger basins of attraction.

</details>


### [287] [Mean-Payoff-Parity and Lifting Strategies from MDPs to 2-Player Stochastic Games](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19324)
*Mohan Dantam,Richard Mayr*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文研究了两人零和回合制随机博弈中最优策略的复杂度（内存和随机化），证明了在shift-invariant inverse-submixing目标下，从MDP到两人博弈需要指数级内存增长的下界，并解决了均值-回报-奇偶性目标的策略复杂度，同时展示了确定性策略的提升方法无法推广到随机化策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解两人零和随机博弈中最优策略所需的内存和随机化复杂度，填补从MDP到博弈场景中策略复杂度下界的理论空白。

Method: 通过构建下界实例证明指数级内存的必要性；针对均值-回报-奇偶性目标，分析其在MDP和随机博弈中的最优策略复杂度差异；构造反例说明确定性策略提升方法不能推广到随机化策略。

Result: (1) 证明了shift-invariant inverse-submixing目标下，从MDP到两人博弈，即使允许随机化策略，指数级内存增长也是必要的；(2) 均值-回报-奇偶性目标在随机博弈中，最优随机化策略需要线性内存（等于偶数颜色数），而非指数级；(3) 存在shift-invariant目标，尽管双方在MDP中都有最优的无记忆随机化策略，但在确定性的两人博弈中，Max的最优随机化策略仍需要无限内存。

Conclusion: 明确了不同目标类下策略复杂度的上下界，揭示了随机化策略在博弈中可能带来比确定性策略更复杂的内存需求，为策略综合与自动化决策提供了理论指导。

Abstract: We consider the strategy complexity (i.e., memory and randomization) of optimal strategies in turn-based 2-player zero-sum stochastic games. Results in [Gimbert,Kelmendi:2023] show how to lift optimal memoryless strategies for shift-invariant inverse-submixing objectives from MDPs to 2-player stochastic games with an exponential increase in the number of memory modes. We show the corresponding lower bound, i.e., the extra exponential memory is required in general, even for randomized strategies. Moreover, we solve the strategy complexity of the well-studied mean-payoff-parity objective in 2-player stochastic games. This objective is also shift-invariant inverse-submixing, but easier than the worst case for this class. In MDPs, Maximizer has optimal memoryless randomized strategies, while optimal deterministic strategies require exponential memory. However, in stochastic games, optimal randomized strategies require, at least and at most, linear memory (equal to the number of even colors). Finally, we show that a different construction for lifting memoryless (resp. finite-memory) deterministic strategies from MDPs (resp. 1-player games) to 2-player games cannot be generalized even to memoryless randomized strategies. We construct a shift-invariant objective where Max and Min each have optimal memoryless randomized strategies in all MDPs, but optimal (randomized) Max strategies still require infinite memory in deterministic 2-player games.

</details>

### [288] [NAVI-Orbital: First In-Orbit Demonstration of a Zero-Shot Vision-Language Model for Autonomous Earth Observation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18271)
*Juan Manuel Delfa Victoria,Taran Cyriac John,Andrew W. Herson*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: NAVI-Orbital在低地球轨道卫星上首次实现了视觉-语言模型的自主多模态推理，通过语义压缩将地球观测从"全部下传"转变为"按需交互"。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 地球观测数据生成速度远超下行带宽和人工处理能力，导致星上采集与地面情报之间存在鸿沟，亟需在轨自主处理能力。

Method: 在LEO卫星上部署Gemma 3视觉-语言模型，利用LangGraph图状态机协调检测与对话智能体，通过自然语言提示替代传统指令序列，实现星上自主分类、描述和对话。

Result: 地面AID基准测试88.16%准确率（7,960张图像），Flatsat验证成功，并在轨实时处理YAM-9原始影像（硬件加速GPU推理，无需微调）。

Conclusion: 在卫星级边缘计算机上运行基础模型是可行的，通过语义压缩改变了传统"全量采集-再下传"的带宽利用模式。

Abstract: As Earth Observation data generation outpaces downlink bandwidth and human-in-the-loop processing, a widening gap has emerged between onboard collection and actionable ground intelligence. This paper presents NAVI-Orbital, a software system deployed on a Low Earth Orbit (LEO) spacecraft. On April 16, 2026, NAVI-Orbital achieved what is, to the authors' knowledge, the first in-orbit demonstration of a vision-language model performing autonomous multi-modal inference entirely onboard. NAVI-Orbital uses a local vision-language model (Gemma 3) to classify each captured scene, produce a text description of its content and the relationships between its features, and respond to operator follow-up via natural-language dialogue. The system is re-tasked through plain-English prompts in place of conventional command sequences, and is orchestrated by a graph-based state machine (LangGraph) coordinating dedicated agents for detection and dialogue. Results across ground benchmarking (88.16% accuracy on the 7,960-image curated AID benchmark), Flatsat validation, and live in-orbit captures of newly acquired, previously unseen Earth imagery (including uncorrected YAM-9 imagery, processed onboard with hardware-accelerated GPU inference and no fine-tuning for the flight instrument) demonstrate the feasibility of running foundation models on satellite-class edge computers to invert the conventional acquire-then-downlink-everything bandwidth profile through semantic compression of Earth observations in-orbit.

### [289] [CaVe-VLM-CoT: An Interpretable Vision-Language Model Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18385)
*Sneha Rao,Shaina Raza,Dhanesh Ramachandram*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: CaVe-VLM-CoT是一个基于反思式智能体RAG的五阶段闭环框架，通过结构化反馈循环强制执行证据支持的推理，显著减少了视觉语言模型中的幻觉问题。该框架在ScienceQA和MMMU上取得了优异性能，并提出了包含23个组件指标和CaVeScore的综合评估体系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VLM存在幻觉问题，即生成流畅但视觉上不忠实的内容。现有的思维链和检索增强方法无法强制步骤级别的引用依据，也无法将验证失败反馈给检索进行修正，因此需要一种能够确保证据支持的闭环推理框架。

Method: 提出了CaVe-VLM-CoT框架，采用五阶段闭环流水线：提取器(Extractor)、检索器(Retriever)、求解器(Solver)、引用注入器(Citation Injector)和验证器(Verifier)。当检测到无依据的声明时，会触发结构化反馈给提取器进行定向重新检索。同时提出了23个跨所有阶段的组件指标和复合指标CaVeScore。

Result: 在ScienceQA上达到87.1%准确率和56.6% CaVeScore；在MMMU（30个主题）上达到55.2%准确率和35.7% CaVeScore。无需任何架构或提示修改。

Conclusion: CaVe-VLM-CoT通过闭环证据推理有效减少了VLM幻觉，同时提供了全面的多维度评估体系，为视觉语言模型的可靠性提升提供了新范式。

Abstract: Vision-Language Models (VLMs) remain prone to hallucinations, producing fluent but visually unfaithful outputs. Existing chain-of-thought and retrieval-augmented methods only partially address this, as they neither enforce step-level citation grounding nor route verification failures back to retrieval for correction. We present CaVe-VLM-CoT, a modular reflection-based agentic-RAG framework that enforces evidence-grounded reasoning through a five-stage closed-loop pipeline: Extractor, Retriever, Solver, Citation Injector, and Verifier, in which detected ungrounded claims trigger structured feedback to the Extractor for targeted re-retrieval. Since no existing framework jointly measures retrieval quality, step-wise citation faithfulness, and cross-modal grounding, we propose a suite of 23 component-wise metrics across all stages, anchored by CaVeScore, a composite metric weighting accuracy, citation precision and recall, attribution, and evidence grounding. Without any architectural or prompt modifications, CaVe-VLM-CoT achieves 87.1\% accuracy and 56.6\% CaVeScore on ScienceQA , and 55.2\% accuracy and 35.7\% CaVeScore on MMMU (30 subjects).

</details>


### [290] [Searching for Synergy in Shared Workspace Human-AI Collaboration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18413)
*Nachiket Kotalwar,Rohini Das,Carolyn Rose*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究共享工作空间中人类-AI团队的协作问题，发现增加协作者若无结构化协调机制会降低性能，而结合共享记忆和模拟人类审批门控的协作框架可提升团队表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管AI代理能力日益增强，但许多科学和专业任务仍需要人类的判断力和情境专业知识，因此需要探索人类与AI如何有效协作。

Method: 使用Collaborative Gym环境与DiscoveryBench任务，通过1,482个会话实验，对比不同团队规模和协作结构（共享群体记忆+模拟人类在环门控）对性能的影响。

Result: 添加相关协作者若缺乏结构化协调会降低性能；提出的协作框架（共享记忆+HITL门控）在三人团队中表现最优，责任信号更清晰，专业知识路由更强。

Conclusion: 人类-AI团队的协调与专业知识整合方式与团队具备的能力同样重要。

Abstract: Automated AI agents are increasingly capable, yet many scientific and professional tasks require human judgment and contextual expertise. We study shared-workspace human-AI teams, where AI agents and human collaborators must coordinate responsibilities before submitting a final answer. Using the Collaborative Gym environment with DiscoveryBench tasks, we examine when adding simulated human collaborators improves performance and when process loss turns additional collaborators into coordination overhead. Across 1,482 sessions, adding relevant collaborators can lower performance when teams lack structure to coordinate their contributions. We then evaluate scaffolding that combines shared group memory with simulated human-in-the-loop (HITL) gates, where selected actions require approval from a designated simulated participant. This scaffolding yields higher mean performance, most clearly in three-person teams, with clearer responsibility signals and stronger routing of expertise to team actions. Overall, how human-AI teams coordinate and integrate expertise matters as much as the capability available to them.

### [291] [CEO-Bench: Can Agents Play the Long Game?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18543)
*Haozhe Chen,Karthik Narasimhan,Zhuang Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: CEO-Bench是一个评估语言模型智能体在长期、不确定、噪声和动态环境中执行复杂任务能力的基准测试，通过模拟经营一家初创公司500天来测试智能体的综合决策能力。最强模型（Claude Opus 4.8和GPT-5.5）也仅能勉强维持初始资金，难以稳定盈利。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有语言模型智能体主要针对短期、孤立任务进行测试，但现实世界中的挑战需要智能体具备长期规划、噪声环境下的信息获取、适应变化世界以及协调多个子目标等综合能力，这些能力尚未得到系统评估。

Method: CEO-Bench通过可编程Python接口模拟一家初创公司的500天运营，智能体需要管理定价、营销、预算等多个方面，处理噪声业务数据库，将信号转化为策略，并通过编程协调大量决策。

Result: 最强智能体虽能编写复杂代码（如模拟客户群体预测现金流、挖掘谈判历史发现隐藏偏好），但多数SOTA模型在该环境中表现挣扎。仅Claude Opus 4.8和GPT-5.5能维持100万美元初始资金以上，且均无法稳定盈利。

Conclusion: CEO-Bench迈出了评估智能体驱动持续、自适应进步所需智能的第一步，揭示了现有语言模型在复杂长期决策任务上的显著不足。

Abstract: Language model agents are becoming proficient executors at isolated, short-horizon tasks such as software engineering and customer service. Yet real-world challenges require a combination of sophisticated skills that remain largely untested in agents: (1) navigating long horizons amid uncertainty; (2) acquiring information in noisy environments; (3) adapting to a changing world; (4) orchestrating multiple moving parts toward a coherent goal. We introduce CEO-Bench, which evaluates these capabilities together by simulating a representative real-world task: operating a startup for 500 days. An agent manages pricing, marketing, budgeting, and many other aspects of a fictional company through a programmable Python interface, operating in the same environment and facing the same challenges as a human CEO. Success demands analyzing noisy, interconnected business databases, translating signals into sound strategy, and coordinating many decisions with programming. The strongest agents write sophisticated code that simulates customer cohorts to forecast future cash and mines negotiation history to uncover hidden customer preferences. Even so, most state-of-the-art models struggle in this environment. Only Claude Opus 4.8 and GPT-5.5 finish above the $1M starting balance, and neither consistently turns a profit. CEO-Bench takes a first step toward measuring the intelligence required to drive sustained, adaptive progress over time.

</details>


### [292] [DeFAb: A Verifiable Benchmark for Defeasible Abduction in Foundation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18557)
*Patrick Cooper,Alvaro Velasquez*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出DeFAb，一个基于四十年公共知识库的形式化溯因推理基准，包含372,648+个实例。规则逻辑求解器可在50微秒内100%准确解决所有实例，而最佳前沿语言模型在鲁棒评估下仅达23.5%。作者还引入DeFAb-Hard和CONJURE（Lean 4/Mathlib的创意变体）。验证器可作为偏好优化的精确奖励。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM在溯因推理中表现不佳，缺乏形式化、可验证的基准来评估模型在"推翻默认规则以解释异常"这一逻辑严谨的创造性推理能力。作者希望用逻辑 rigor 作为衡量创造力和理论推理的工具。

Method: 结合四种知识库（OpenCyc, YAGO, Wikidata的分类层级 + ConceptNet, UMLS的行为属性图），生成372,648+个溯因推理实例。每个假设必须通过多项式时间验证（有效推导、保守性、最小性）。包含三个难度级别，以及DeFAb-Hard变体和CONJURE（Lean 4形式化创意变体）。

Result: 规则逻辑求解器50微秒内100%准确；最佳LLM在鲁棒评估下仅23.5%（Level 2为7.8-23.5%）；思维链方差(~36 pp)超过模型间差距；污染对照显示+19.4 pp的Level 3差距。CONJURE试点发现零个新颖概念。

Conclusion: 前沿LLM未能可靠内化可废止推理；形式化验证作为奖励信号是可行的（DPO, RLVR/GRPO）；当前模型在真正的逻辑创造性推理上仍有根本性局限。

Abstract: A rule-based logic solver resolves every instance in our benchmark in under 50 microseconds with 100% accuracy; the best frontier language model reaches 65% at best and drops to 23.5% under rendering-robust evaluation (worst case over four surface renderings). We introduce DeFAb (Defeasible Abduction Benchmark), a dataset and generation pipeline that converts four decades of publicly funded knowledge bases into formally grounded instances for defeasible abduction: constructing hypotheses that explain anomalies by overriding defaults while preserving unrelated expectations. Because every hypothesis must pass polynomial-time checks for valid derivation, conservativity, and minimality, DeFAb makes logical rigor the instrument for measuring creativity and theoretical reasoning, scoring the disciplined construction of theory revisions rather than fluent but theory-destroying prose. The pipeline pairs taxonomic hierarchies (OpenCyc, YAGO, Wikidata) with behavioral property graphs (ConceptNet, UMLS) to produce 372,648+ instances across 33.75M materialized rules from 18 sources, in three levels with polynomial-time verifiable gold standards. Four frontier models do not reliably internalize defeasible reasoning: rendering-robust Level 2 accuracy is 7.8-23.5%; chain-of-thought variance (~36 pp) exceeds any inter-model gap; and a matched contamination control isolates a +19.4 pp Level 3 gap. We further release DeFAb-Hard (a 235-instance Level 3 difficulty variant; best model 53.3% vs 100% symbolic) and CONJURE (a kernel-verified transformative-creativity variant of 560 Lean 4/Mathlib instances whose gold answers are definitions the proof kernel did not previously contain, judge-free verifier; a pilot finds zero novel concepts). The same verifier doubles as an exact reward for preference optimization (DPO, RLVR/GRPO). Released under MIT at https://huggingface.co/datasets/PatrickAllenCooper/DeFAb.

</details>


### [293] [Optimizing Lithium Production Decisions under Geological, Demand, and Pricing Uncertainties: A POMDP Framework for Multi-Objective Decision Making](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18598)
*Anna C. Edmonds,Mansur M. Arief,Robert J. Moss,Mykel J. Kochenderfer,Jef Caers*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出将锂矿开采决策问题建模为部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程(POMDP)，通过信念状态规划方法求解，在多种价格机制和矿床场景下，相比人工启发式策略能更动态地适应价格变化，实现更高的需求满足率和更平衡的经济环境效益。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 锂生产决策面临地质不确定性、价格不确定性和多种提取技术选择等挑战，现有模型未能同时考虑定价不确定性、需求不确定性及不同开采技术，导致难以制定稳健的开采策略。

Method: 将锂矿决策问题建模为部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程(POMDP)，采用信念状态规划方法求解，在静态、线性、指数和随机四种价格机制下比较POMDP求解器与人工启发式策略的表现。

Result: POMDP求解器在所有价格和矿床场景下均优于人工启发式策略，通过信念状态规划和显式不确定性管理动态适应价格变化，实现了更高的需求满足率和更均衡的经济环境结果。

Conclusion: 将定价模型和提取技术纳入决策框架，通过POMDP方法优化开采顺序、生产和技术选择，能够获得更稳健的锂矿决策策略。

Abstract: Decision making in lithium production is challenging, whether from an investor's perspective or a strategic production standpoint. Determining which mines to open and when to open them involves not only geological and price uncertainties, but also complexities around the choice of extraction method, from direct lithium extraction to hard rock mining. Prior work explored models of this problem and different methods to optimize mining decisions; these models did not account for uncertainty in pricing, uncertainty in demand, or different mining technologies to extract lithium. Incorporating different pricing models and extraction technology into these models enables more robust strategies for determining not only when and where to open a mine, but also which method of production to pursue. We frame the problem as a partially observable Markov decision process (POMDP) and solve using belief state planning methods to get optimal decision making. In our study, we show that POMDP solvers outperform human inspired heuristics by dynamically adapting to shifting lithium price regimes (static, linear, exponential, and stochastic) through belief state planning and explicit uncertainty management. By optimally sequencing exploration, production, and technology choice, the framework achieves higher demand fulfillment and more balanced economic environmental outcomes over the projects lifetime in all different pricing and deposit scenarios.

Because the world is simulated, the same setup can generate continuous or binary forecasting questions at arbitrary time horizons, paired intervention worlds for conditional or causal questions, and resolved examples of rare or disruptive outcomes. Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文为通用型智能体建立了形式化记忆理论，证明当两个领域存在观察瓶颈但需要不相容的最优动作时，任何近似最优策略都必须在瓶颈处诱导出不同的记忆分布，并进一步证明如果记忆包含足够信息，可用于近似重建局部转移动力学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解通用型智能体在面对多个环境和目标时，为什么必须依赖记忆而非仅靠当前观察，以及记忆在其中扮演的具体角色。

Method: 通过形式化分析，定义"观察瓶颈"概念，证明分离定理：当领域共享观察瓶颈但最优动作不相容时，近似最优策略必须在该瓶颈处维持不同的记忆分布。进一步证明记忆与价值估计、转移动力学重建之间的关系。

Result: 证明了分离定理：成功的通用型智能体不能仅依赖当前状态观察，必须保存领域相关信息于记忆中。同时证明了包含足够信息的记忆可用于近似重建局部转移动力学。

Conclusion: 记忆是支撑通用型智能体实现领域区分、转移模型重建和规划的核心基础。

Abstract: This paper develops a formal account of what generalist agents must store in memory in order to act near-optimally across multiple environments and goals. It shows that when two domains share an observational bottleneck but require incompatible optimal actions, any uniformly near-optimal policy must induce distinct memory distributions at that bottleneck. The result yields a separation theorem: sufficiently successful agents cannot rely only on current state observations, but must preserve domain-relevant information in memory. The paper further shows that if an agent's memory contains enough information to estimate values for related goals, then that memory can be used to approximately reconstruct the agent's local transition dynamics. Together, these results characterize memory as the substrate that supports domain disambiguation, transition-model reconstruction, and planning for generalist agents.

TL;DR: 本文提出ProfiLLM，一个面向工业级网约车调度系统的智能体LLM数据流水线，通过工具增强的全局知识挖掘和效用对齐的画像探索两个模块，将LLM作为语义特征提取器从海量行为日志中生成用户画像，在滴滴实际部署中取得了显著的AUC、GMV和完成率提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 工业级网约车调度系统仍主要依赖结构化数值特征，但许多关键行为信号（如司机对特定区域的习惯性回避）本质上具有上下文语义，适合用LLM生成用户画像来表达。然而，将LLM扩展到毫秒级延迟的生产调度系统中面临三大挑战：日志远超LLM上下文窗口、长尾用户交互稀疏、表面流畅的画像未必改善下游预测效用。

Conclusion: ProfiLLM证明了将LLM作为语义特征提取器集成到工业级网约车调度系统的可行性和有效性，通过知识挖掘和效用对齐的策略成功克服了规模化部署中的上下文窗口限制、长尾用户稀疏性和效用对齐等关键挑战。

However, scaling such profiling to a live, millisecond-latency dispatcher faces three intertwined constraints rarely addressed together: on a platform with millions of daily orders, logs exceed any LLM's context window by orders of magnitude; most users are long-tail, with too few interactions for per-user profiling; and surface-fluent profiles do not necessarily improve downstream prediction utility. We present ProfiLLM, an agentic LLM data pipeline that operationalizes utility-aligned user profiling for production matching systems through two modules. (1) Tool-Augmented Global Knowledge Mining equips an LLM agent with 27 analytical tools to mine platform-scale data, producing reusable global knowledge, adaptive user clustering rules, and region-level supply-demand priors. (2) Utility-Aligned Profile Exploration generates multiple candidate profiles per cluster, evaluates them via a lightweight downstream utility proxy, iteratively refines the best candidates and constructs preference pairs for DPO fine-tuning. Deployed on DiDi's production dispatcher, ProfiLLM achieves up to +6.14% relative AUC improvement in outcome prediction, up to +4.35% GMV gain in dispatching simulation, and consistent improvements in a 14-day online A/B test including +0.47% GMV, +0.33% Completion Rate, and -0.82% Cancel-Before-Accept rate.

Method: Xcientist将文献证据、想法状态、实现计划、消融记录和修复痕迹作为持久化研究制品，通过合约约束的流程将研究综合与实验验证外部化，确保生成机制可落地、可测试、可修订，且不丢失其证据基础。

Abstract: AI systems can increasingly automate scientific workflows, but the reasoning that links prior evidence, generated ideas, experiments and final claims often remains implicit inside model inference. Xcientist organizes literature evidence, idea states, implementation plans, ablation records and repair traces as persistent research artifacts, so that generated mechanisms can be grounded, executed, tested and revised without losing their evidential basis. We identify claim drift as a failure mode of automated research, where runnable artifacts no longer support the mechanism originally claimed. Across training-free memory systems, graph-structured traffic forecasting and multi-scale physics-informed neural networks, Xcientist preserves traceable trajectories from problem formulation to mechanism design, validation and bounded revision. These results suggest that AI scientists should be evaluated not only by their final artifacts, but by whether their synthesis and validation processes remain attributable, inspectable and scientifically accountable.

### [300] [Decoupling Search from Reasoning: A Vendor-Agnostic Grounding Architecture for LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18947)
*Emmanuel Aboah Boateng,Kyle MacDonald,Amardeep Kumar,Siddharth Kodwani,Sudeep Das*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出解耦式搜索增强（DSG），将搜索过程从推理模型中分离出来，通过MCP兼容网关实现独立控制。实验表明DSG在保持接近原生搜索精度的同时，可降低91%-98%的搜索成本、提升缓存命中率至99.4%、降低68%延迟，并避免搜索诱导的冗长输出问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出Decoupled Search Grounding (DSG)框架，采用供应商无关的架构，通过MCP兼容网关将搜索接地移出推理模型。DSG提供提供商路由、来源感知上下文渲染、配置化回退、检索深度控制、精确与语义缓存等一流的独立控制能力。

Conclusion: 实时搜索接地应被视为可优化的接口边界，而非固定的模型特征。DSG证明了通过解耦设计能在保持甚至提升精度的同时，大幅降低成本和延迟，提升系统的可控性与可移植性。

Abstract: Production LLM agents increasingly depend on real-time search, yet native search grounding bundles retrieval policy, provider choice, evidence injection, cost, latency, and generation behavior behind a single model-provider boundary. This coupling makes grounding hard to inspect, tune, reuse, or port, and can trigger Search-Induced Verbosity that breaks strict output contracts. We present Decoupled Search Grounding (DSG), a vendor-agnostic boundary that moves grounding outside the reasoning model through an MCP-compatible gateway, exposing provider routing, source-aware context rendering, configured fallback, retrieval-depth control, and exact plus semantic caching as first-class controls. Across five frontier models on SimpleQA, FreshQA, and HotpotQA, native search leads on recency-sensitive FreshQA, but DSG exposes a stronger frontier when control matters: on SimpleQA it nearly matches native accuracy (86.1% vs. 87.7%) at 91% lower search cost, preserves concise answer contracts, and reaches a 99.4% warm-cache hit rate with 68% lower latency. Deployed as a shared production grounding layer for large-scale agentic workloads with interchangeable models, DSG matches or slightly exceeds native-search accuracy on an e-commerce query-understanding (QIU) workload while cutting search cost by over 98%. Real-time grounding is best treated as an optimizable interface boundary, not a fixed model feature.

### [301] [Generative-Model Predictive Planning for Navigation in Partially Observable Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18888)
*Thomas Quilter,Yifan Zhu,Guorui Quan,Mingfei Sun,Samuel Kaski*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: BeliefDiffusion结合扩散模型表征多模态信念分布与MPC规划，在部分可观测环境中显著优于强化学习和生成式方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Navigation in partially observable environments presents a significant challenge for autonomous agents, requiring effective decision-making with limited sensory information in unknown environments. Belief-based methods, particularly those using neural networks to approximate the belief space, often fail to capture the inherent multimodality of belief spaces, especially in high-dimensional cases with perceptual aliasing. While generative models present a compelling alternative, they typically require substantial data or expert demonstrations and lack explicit mechanisms for long-term planning. In this paper, we introduce BeliefDiffusion, a novel framework that combines the benefits of both generation and planning. BeliefDiffusion leverages diffusion models to explicitly characterize multimodal belief distributions and utilizes Model Predictive Control (MPC) to simultaneously plan ahead. It consists of two steps: (1) Imagining plausible environment configurations based on observation history and (2) Planning efficient navigation strategies across an aggregated configurations. Through extensive experiments in synthetic map environments, we demonstrate that BeliefDiffusion significantly outperforms both model-free reinforcement learning baselines and other generative approaches in navigation success rate and path efficiency. Our results validate that explicitly incorporating multimodal belief representations into planning enables more robust navigation in partially observable settings.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有GUI智能体依赖专家轨迹的行为克隆，但闭环执行中策略会偏离专家策略，进入专家轨迹未覆盖的离轨状态，这些状态缺乏有效监督，导致策略无法选择正确动作。

Method: SGCD框架：1) 先让无技能策略运行几步到达真实的离轨状态；2) 从这些状态出发，用技能引导策略完成任务并生成成功延续轨迹；3) 将延续轨迹与专家轨迹混合，为离轨状态提供监督；4) 技能从成功和失败的rollout中提取，包括延续计划、关键目标、失败陷阱和成功标准。

Result: 在OSWorld-Verified基准上，SGCD将三个基础模型（均为30%左右）的成功率提升至50%以上，证明了方法的有效性和泛化能力。

Conclusion: SGCD通过技能引导的延续蒸馏有效解决了专家轨迹监督覆盖不足的问题，是一种通用且有效的GUI智能体自我改进框架。

Abstract: Improving GUI agents typically relies on behavior cloning on expert trajectories. However, as the current policy deviates from the expert policy, it inevitably encounters policy-induced off-trajectory states during closed-loop execution, i.e., states that fall outside the expert trajectories. Since expert trajectories provide no demonstrations for these unseen states, such states receive no effective supervision, leaving the policy unable to select the correct action. To close this supervision gap, we propose Skill-Guided Continuation Distillation (SGCD), an iterative self-improvement framework. SGCD first runs the plain policy without skill guidance for a few steps to reach realistic off-trajectory states. From these states, a skill-guided policy then completes the task and produces successful continuations, which are mixed with expert trajectories to supply supervision over policy-induced off-trajectory states. The skills are extracted from both successful and failed rollouts, consisting of Continuation Plans, Critical Targets, Failure Traps, and Success Criteria. On OSWorld-Verified, SGCD improves the success rate of three base models from the low-30\% range to over 50\%, demonstrating its effectiveness and generality.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

By innovatively coupling this dynamic curriculum scheduler with a multi dimensional, process aware reward mechanism and a reflective learning paradigm, we significantly elevate the model's overall reasoning quality. Extensive experiments on mainstream benchmarks demonstrate that ThinkDeception establishes a new SOTA, significantly outperforming existing methods in both detection accuracy and rationale quality. Ultimately, this work successfully drives the field of deception detection toward interpretable, multimodal cognitive reasoning.

### [306] [RODS: Reward-Driven Online Data Synthesis for Multi-Turn Tool-Use Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19047)
*Ruishan Fang,Siyuan Lu,Chenyi Zhuang,Tao Lin*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出RODS方法，通过奖励方差检测能力边界并在线合成数据，解决多轮工具使用强化学习中静态数据集信息样本快速耗尽的问题，以20倍少的轨迹达到与17K样本离线管道相当的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多轮工具使用的强化学习受限于静态数据集中信息样本的快速耗尽。GRPO的梯度信号集中在能力边界处的任务上，随着训练推进，静态数据集中这些信息样本逐渐耗尽，导致训练瓶颈。

Method: 提出RODS（Reward-driven Online Data Synthesis），利用进度奖励方差作为零成本的边界检测器，持续识别能力边界样本；通过技能对齐的重采样管道合成结构复杂度匹配的多轮变体；管理一个与策略共演化的动态回放缓冲区。

Result: 从400个人工种子样本出发，仅维持约800个活跃训练样本，RODS即可达到与17K样本离线管道相当的性能，轨迹需求减少约20倍；在受控环境下优于固定数据RL和环境增强方法。

Conclusion: RODS通过在线数据合成有效解决了静态数据集信息样本耗尽的问题，显著提升了数据效率，为多轮工具使用强化学习提供了一种实用且高效的范式。

Abstract: Multi-turn tool-use RL is bottlenecked by the rapid depletion of informative samples in static datasets. We observe that the gradient signal in GRPO concentrates on tasks with the highest rollout reward variance, a consequence of the Popoviciu upper bound. Consequently, samples near the agent's capability boundary -- where successes and failures are roughly balanced -- contribute disproportionately large policy gradients. As training progresses, this boundary continuously shifts, which gradually depletes the pool of informative samples in a static dataset. We propose RODS (Reward-driven Online Data Synthesis) to resolve this depletion. RODS closes the loop between RL training and data generation by repurposing the progress reward variance as a practical, zero-cost boundary detector that requires no extra inference beyond the rollouts already computed for training. It continuously identifies such boundary samples, synthesizes new multi-turn variants matching their structural complexity (e.g., API topology and dependency depth) via a skill-aligned resampling pipeline, and manages a dynamic replay buffer that co-evolves with the policy. Starting from 400 human seeds and maintaining an active training pool of ~800 samples, RODS achieves comparable performance to a 17K-sample offline pipeline while requiring roughly 20x fewer trajectories, and improves over fixed-data RL and environment augmentation in our controlled setting.

### [307] [ARIADNE: Agnostic Routing for Inference-time Adapter DyNamic sElection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19079)
*Enrico Cassano,Michał Brzozowski,Zuzanna Dubanowska,Paolo Mandica,Neo Christopher Chung*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出ARIADNE，一种无需训练、与适配器无关的推理时动态适配器选择框架，通过在嵌入空间中计算适配器训练数据的质心，实现无任务标签情况下的适配器自动路由，在23个NLP任务上达到97.44%的上限性能恢复。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有PEFT模型生态中，多个任务专用适配器共享一个骨干模型，推理时查询常缺少任务标签。现有路由方法要么依赖适配器内部结构（如权重分解、梯度统计），要么需要额外训练路由器，难以随新适配器扩展。

Method: ARIADNE为每个适配器从其训练集嵌入中计算一组质心，以捕捉该适配器的数据分布。推理时对于无标签输入，通过测量输入嵌入与这些质心在潜在空间中的距离来选择适配器。路由完全在输入嵌入空间中进行，无需修改适配器或训练过程。

Result: 在Llama 3.2 1B Instruct上评估23个NLP任务，恢复97.44%的上限性能。扩展到44个任务时，平均选择准确率达到89.7%。

Conclusion: ARIADNE是一种训练无关、适配器无关的高效路由框架，兼容任意PEFT方法，无需适配器内部信息或额外训练，具有良好的可扩展性和可移植性。

Abstract: The increasing deployment of parameter-efficient fine-tuning (PEFT) has led to model ecosystems in which a single backbone is paired with many task-specialized adapters. In this setting, inference-time queries often arrive without task labels, requiring the system to automatically select the most appropriate adapter from a growing and heterogeneous adapter pool. Existing routing methods either depend on access to adapter internals, such as weight decompositions or gradient-based statistics, or require additional router training, which limits scalability and portability as new adapters are added. We introduce ARIADNE, a training-free, adapter-agnostic routing framework for dynamic adapter selection at inference time. ARIADNE represents each adapter through a set of centroids computed from embeddings of its training set, capturing the data distribution associated with that adapter. Given an unlabeled input, it selects an adapter by measuring proximity to these centroids in latent space. Because routing is performed entirely in the input embedding space, ARIADNE is compatible with arbitrary PEFT methods and requires no modification to the adapters or training procedures. Primarily evaluated with Llama 3.2 1B Instruct on 23 diverse NLP tasks, ARIADNE recovers 97.44% of the upper bound performance. Scaling to 44 tasks, it achieves 89.7% average selection accuracy, without additional training or access to adapter internals.

### [308] [Towards an Agent-First Web: Redesigning the Web for AI Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19116)
*Eranga Bandara,Ross Gore,Ravi Mukkamala,Asanga Gunaratna,Safdar H. Bouk,Xueping Liang,Peter Foytik,Abdul Rahman,Sachini Rajapakse,Isurunima Kularathna,Pramoda Karunarathna,Chalani Rajapakse,Ng Wee Keong,Kasun De Zoysa,Tharaka Hewa,Amin Hass,Wathsala Herath,Aruna Withanage,Nilaan Loganathan,Atmaram Yarlagadda,Sachin Shetty*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出，随着AI代理成为人类与Web内容之间的中介，原有的"内容消费者是人"这一核心假设已被打破。作者从访问层、经济层和内容层三个层面提出了十项设计原则，旨在将AI代理重构为Web的"一等公民"，包括代理继承人类访问权限、基于意图的分层经济模型，以及提出ATML标记语言和加密溯源链来应对"认知递归"问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Web架构基于"人类是内容主要消费者"这一过时假设，导致AI代理被大量屏蔽、歧视性排除，且经济模型将代理访问视为"掠夺"而非合法交互。这种对抗性关系无法持续，亟需从底层重新设计Web的社会契约。

Method: 提出了三层十项设计原则：(1) 访问层——代理应继承人类同等访问权限，引入速率限制、代理标识元数据（类似浏览器头信息）和双架构内容分发（人类可读+代理优化）；(2) 经济层——基于"代理即人类代理人"原则的意图分层框架，提出代币订阅模型和委托内容经济；(3) 内容层——识别"认知递归"（AI生成内容被代理消费并再生成，逐步脱离人类真实知识）问题，提出ATML四层人类监督模型和加密溯源链。

Result: 系统性地提出了一个面向AI代理的Web重构框架，包含三个层面共十条设计原则，并给出了ATML这一具体技术方案来应对内容层面"认知递归"带来的知识真实性危机。

Conclusion: 我们需要重新谈判Web的基础社会契约，将AI代理从被排斥者转变为Web的"一等公民"。这种重构不是技术微调，而是对Web访问、经济和内容层根本规则的重新设计。

Abstract: The World Wide Web was built on an assumption held for three decades: the primary consumer of web content is a human being. This permeates every layer; its access model presumes human visitors, its economics rest on human attention, and its content targets human perception. The rapid emergence of AI agents as intermediaries between humans and web content invalidates this assumption. Yet the web resists agents through blanket blocking, CAPTCHA-based exclusion, and economic models that treat agent access as extraction rather than legitimate interaction.
  This paper proposes a principled redesign across three layers. At the access layer, agents acting for humans should inherit equivalent access rights, governed by rate limiting and agent identification metadata in HTTP requests, analogous to browser headers, alongside a dual-layer architecture serving human-readable and agent-optimized content from the same domain. At the economic layer, we propose an intent-based tier framework grounded in the agent-as-human-proxy principle: an agent's economic obligation mirrors that of the human it represents. A token-based subscription model meters content in tokens rather than pageviews, alongside a commissioned content economy anchoring AI content production in human intentionality. At the content layer, we identify epistemic recursion, the self-referential loop in which AI-generated content is consumed by agents to produce further content, progressively detaching web knowledge from human ground truth. We propose the Agent Text Markup Language (ATML), a four-level human supervision tier model, and a cryptographic provenance chain to counter this threat.
  Together these constitute ten design principles for an agent-first internet, one in which agents are first-class citizens whose integration requires renegotiating the web's foundational social contract across access, economics, and content.

</details>

Abstract: Electricity markets are inherently complex systems characterised by strong nonlinearities, high-dimensional interactions, and increasing interdependence across regions. This paper addresses this gap by combining DNN models with explainable artificial intelligence (XAI) techniques to analyse the determinants of electricity prices across 39 European bidding zones. Gas prices remain a dominant and consistent driver across electricity markets, while interconnections significantly shape price dynamics, highlighting the strong interdependence of European electricity systems. ### [310] [Human-AI Coevolution Dynamics: A Formal Theory of Social Intelligence Emergence Through Long-Term Interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19144)

Method: 提出HACD-H框架，整合情感适应、关系组织、社会记忆和人格一致性；构建约14,700轮对话数据集；设计理论驱动的实证评估框架。

Result: 发现了社会认知的时间持久性层级结构、稳定的关系吸引子、相变式发展模式以及结构化的社会认知能量景观；社会智能与社会认知能量呈显著负相关（r=-0.391, p<0.001）；交互轨迹随时间呈现能量递减趋势。

Conclusion: 社会智能源于长期社会认知共演，HACD-H为建模自适应人机社会交互和发展社会智能AI系统提供了统一理论基础。

Abstract: Current conversational AI systems have made significant progress in language generation, personalization, and long-context interaction. However, most existing methods model social behavior through isolated components such as emotion modeling, memory retrieval, or persona conditioning, lacking a unified framework to explain the emergence of stable social relationships and social intelligence in long-term human-AI interaction.To address this, we propose the Human-AI Coevolution Dynamics Framework (HACD-H), a formal model of human-AI interaction as a self-organizing social cognitive system. HACD-H integrates emotional adaptation, relational organization, social memory, and personality consistency into a unified dynamical framework and introduces principles including multi-timescale social cognition, relational attractors, trust basins, developmental phase transitions, and social cognitive energy dynamics.We construct a conversational dataset with approximately 14,700 interaction turns and develop a theory-driven empirical evaluation framework. Results reveal a hierarchy of temporal persistence in social cognition, stable relational attractors, phase-transition-like developmental patterns, and a structured social cognitive energy landscape. Social intelligence shows a significant negative correlation with social cognitive energy (r = -0.391, p < 0.001), and interaction trajectories exhibit progressive energy reduction over time.These findings suggest that social intelligence emerges from long-term social cognitive coevolution rather than isolated conversational capabilities. HACD-H provides a unified theoretical foundation for modeling adaptive human-AI social interaction and developing socially intelligent AI systems.

</details>


### [311] [Beyond Safe Data: Pretraining-Stage Alignment with Regular Safety Reflection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19168)
*Jinhan Li,Kexian Tang,Yihan Xu,Zhuorui Ye,Kaifeng Lyu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出安全反思预训练方法，在预训练阶段将安全反思文本插入语料库，使LLM在语言建模中内建自我监控能力，相比数据过滤和重写，能更有效地防止模型从安全数据中泛化出不安全行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的预训练阶段安全对齐方法主要关注数据层面的安全（过滤或改写不安全数据），但忽略了模型可能从看似安全的知识和能力中组合出不安全行为，因此需要更根本的行为塑造。

Method: 在预训练语料中定期插入简短的"安全反思"文本，使模型在语言建模过程中直接内建自我监控能力，再通过兼容的后训练强化这一基础能力。

Result: 在1.7B模型上，该方法提升了安全分类准确率，显著降低了推理阶段和微调攻击的成功率。在合成环境MedSafetyWorld中，相比数据过滤和重写，该方法在防止模型从安全数据中泛化出不安全行为方面表现更优。

Conclusion: 预训练阶段的对齐不仅要确保训练数据安全，更要主动塑造模型可能从安全数据中习得的行为模式。

Abstract: To achieve deeper safety alignment for large language models (LLMs), recent efforts have studied how to push safety interventions earlier into the pretraining stage, primarily by filtering unsafe data or rewriting it into safer forms. We argue that pretraining-stage alignment should go beyond making the data safe: LLMs may compose seemingly benign knowledge and capabilities into unsafe behaviors. To this end, we propose Safety Reflection Pretraining, a pretraining-stage alignment method which regularly inserts short safety reflections into pretraining corpora to integrate self-monitoring directly into language modeling, establishing a foundational capability that is subsequently reinforced by compatible post-training. Our experiments with 1.7B models pretrained on FineWeb-Edu show that Safety Reflection Pretraining improves safety classification accuracy and substantially reduces the success rates of inference-stage and finetuning attacks. Complementary to our real-world experiments, we also introduce a fully controlled synthetic environment, MedSafetyWorld, with a clear definition of safety and a reasoning structure under which models can easily generalize unsafe behaviors from safe data. Ablations in MedSafetyWorld further demonstrate a clear advantage of Safety Reflection Pretraining in preventing models from acting on unsafe behaviors generalized from safe data, compared with data filtering and rewriting. Taken together, our findings suggest that pretraining alignment should not only make the training data safe, but also shape the behaviors that models are likely to acquire from safe data.

### [312] [User as Engram: Internalizing Per-User Memory as Local Parametric Edits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19172)
*Bojie Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出"用户即记忆印迹"(User as Engram)方法，将用户个性化内容以手术级精确方式写入模型的哈希键控记忆表，用共享适配器承载推理能力，实现了比LoRA更优的间接推理准确率（平均提升5.6倍）和极小的内存占用（约33,000倍更小）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法如LoRA将用户事实作为全局权重增量写入，把"内容"与"推理技能"混为一谈，导致污染无关文本且内存效率低下。作者受大脑记忆机制启发（海马体存稀疏局部印迹、新皮层存共享技能），希望将个性化中的内容存储与推理技能分离。

Method: 采用分层设计：1) 内容层：将用户事实以手术级编辑写入Engram模型的哈希键控记忆表（加法叠加，不改变其他位置）；2) 推理层：使用共享适配器承载推理能力。不同用户的事实占据不重叠的哈希槽，支持无损叠加共存。

Result: 1) 直接回忆能力与LoRA持平；2) 间接推理准确率平均提升5.6倍；3) 无任何用户在推理能力上低于基座模型；4) 内存占用缩小约33,000倍；5) 支持多用户无损共存；6) 约100个事实后优于带检索管线的2.5倍大模型。

Conclusion: User as Engram通过模仿大脑的记忆分离机制，将个性化中的"内容存储"与"推理技能"解耦，在性能、内存效率和可扩展性上全面优于现有方法，是一种更优雅、更高效的用户个性化方案。

Abstract: Personal memory in a language model is two problems: content and reasoning skill. The brain keeps the two apart (a sparse, local engram in the hippocampus for each episode, a slow neocortex for the shared skills that interpret it), so a new fact need not overwrite everything else. Most personalization today keeps a user's facts outside the weights, in a natural-language memory file or a retrieval index. When facts are written into the model instead, the standard recipe is the per-user LoRA adapter, which does the opposite of the brain, folding content and skill into one global weight delta. Writing a user's facts as a LoRA contaminates text unrelated to them; writing the same facts as local Engram rows leaves it mathematically untouched, resulting in a roughly 33,000x smaller memory footprint.
  We therefore propose User as Engram: store a user's content as surgical edits to the hash-keyed memory table of an Engram model, and carry the reasoning skill in one shared adapter. This layered design matches per-user LoRA's direct recall while delivering 5.6x higher indirect-reasoning accuracy on average, and never makes a single user worse at reasoning than the untouched base. The edit is a glass box: writing a fact switches on its lookup at exactly the trigger, adds the value the answer needs, leaves every other position unchanged to the last bit, and fails if written into the wrong layer. Because different users' facts land in disjoint hash slots, their edits compose: many users live in one shared table at once, stacking additively and losslessly, where a per-user LoRA, a single global weight delta, admits only one. Upon retrieval, a per-user Engram table does not grow with the population the retriever must search, so past ~100 facts it overtakes a retrieval pipeline on a 2.5x larger model.

</details>

*Hannah Le,Ramesh Ramasamy,Alex Urrutia,Mahsa Yazdani,Tim Proctor,Kenny Workman*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI智能体有望加速药物发现，但实际部署需要在真实的程序性决策场景中进行可信评估。现有评估多依赖文献中的记忆化事实，缺乏对真实世界实验数据的解读能力测试。

Method: 构建TxBench-PP基准测试，包含100个评估任务，涵盖作用机制、药效学推理、化合物-靶点结合、因果靶点验证、可开发性与安全性、转化疗效等多个维度。智能体接收真实工作流快照，在编码环境中检查文件并返回结构化答案，通过确定性方式进行评分。

Result: 在16种模型配置、11个模型和4,800条轨迹中，最强配置Claude Opus 4.8/Pi仅通过59.3%的测试（178/300），GPT-5.5/Pi为55.3%（166/300），没有任何系统能可靠地恢复临床前药理学决策。

Conclusion: 现有AI智能体在临床前药理学决策任务上表现有限，无法可靠地替代人类专家进行真实的药物研发决策，该基准测试为后续AI药物发现系统的改进提供了重要的评估标准。

Abstract: Artificial intelligence (AI) agents promise to accelerate drug discovery by compressing interpretation and decision-making loops, but practical deployment requires trusted evaluation on realistic program decisions. We introduce TherapeuticsBench Preclinical Pharmacology (TxBench-PP), a verifiable benchmark for small-molecule preclinical pharmacology and the first focused slice of a broader TherapeuticsBench effort across drug-discovery stages and therapeutic modalities. TxBench-PP tests whether agents can recover accurate conclusions from real-world assay data rather than memorized facts from literature. The benchmark contains 100 evaluations indexed by program stage, assay type, and task structure, spanning mechanism-of-action (MoA) and pharmacodynamic (PD) reasoning, compound-target engagement, causal target validation, developability and safety, and translational efficacy. Agents receive realistic workflow snapshots, inspect files in a coding environment, and return structured answers graded deterministically. Across 16 model-harness configurations, comprising 11 models and 4,800 trajectories, no system reliably recovered preclinical pharmacology decisions. The strongest configuration, Claude Opus 4.8 / Pi, passed 59.3\% of endpoint attempts (178/300; 95\% CI, 51.1-67.6), followed by GPT-5.5 / Pi at 55.3\% (166/300; 47.0-63.6).

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建X+Slides基准：涵盖113个主题和7种演讲场景，设计8,133个去重且源验证的探针，为同一探针分配不同的受众特定效用权重，提出四个互补指标（受众覆盖度、领域覆盖度、效率、正确性）。

Result: 在τ_A=0.7阈值下，DeepPresenter最佳受众覆盖度0.714，SlideTailor为0.594，NotebookLM消融实验达0.853但存在明显接地性差异。

Abstract: Automatically generating slide decks from source documents is an important application of large language models (LLMs). Existing benchmarks primarily assess slide completeness and technical depth, while overlooking the target audience as a critical real-world factor. For instance, specialists demand rigorous proofs, whereas decision-makers prioritize actionable conclusions. To bridge this gap, we introduce X+Slides, a benchmark specifically designed for audience-conditioned slide generation. Built on a diverse corpus spanning 113 topics and seven presentation scenes, X+Slides employs a dynamic evaluation framework constructed from 8,133 deduplicated, source-grounded probes. By assigning audience-specific utility weights to the same source-grounded probes, X+Slides reports four complementary metrics: Audience Coverage measures how much audience-essential information is conveyed, Domain-wise Coverage shows which information types are covered, Efficiency measures delivered utility per unit of attention cost, and Correctness verifies whether slide claims are supported by the source. Experiments on DeepPresenter, SlideTailor, and NotebookLM show that current systems can recover a substantial but still incomplete part of audience-essential information: at $τ_A=0.7$, DeepPresenter reaches a best Audience Coverage of 0.714, SlideTailor reaches 0.594, and the NotebookLM ablation reaches 0.853 while showing clear grounding differences. These results indicate that visual quality and broad topic coverage should not be treated as evidence support without source-grounded evaluation.

### [315] [NeSyCat Torch: A Differentiable Tensor Implementation of Categorical Semantics for Neurosymbolic Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19279)
*Daniel Romero Schellhorn,Till Mossakowski,Björn Gehrke*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出NeSyCat Torch框架，通过单子（monad）参数化统一了神经符号语义的多种范式（经典、模糊、概率、神经），使用分布单子、懒对数张量单子和批处理单子实现高效可微训练，在MNIST加法任务上优于LTN和DeepProbLog，接近DeepStochLog性能，且保持统一的框架通用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 神经符号语义存在碎片化问题，经典、模糊、概率和神经系统各自定义真值的归纳规则不同。现有的NeSyCat框架虽然能通过强单子和聚合结构统一这些范式，但缺乏对神经网络学习的谓词和函数的解释能力。

Method: 提出NeSyCat Torch框架，通过神经网络解释计算符号，在概率编程和张量后端实现。使用分布单子作为参考语义和度量评估，引入懒对数张量单子（基于对数半环）实现数值稳定且可微的训练，采用批处理单子支持批量高效训练。公理作为源代码，基于单子的do-notation一次编写，单子绑定自动执行边缘化和懒惰剪枝。

Result: 在MNIST加法任务上，HaskTorch、JAX和PyTorch实现在速度和准确率上均优于LTN和DeepProbLog，准确率接近DeepStochLog。保持了统一框架的通用性，可应用于多种一阶神经符号方法。

Conclusion: NeSyCat Torch成功连接了NeSyCat框架与神经网络学习，通过单子参数化实现了统一的神经符号语义框架。未来工作可扩展至连续概率（如Giry单子）的神经表示。

Abstract: Neurosymbolic semantics is fragmented: classical, fuzzy, probabilistic and neural systems each define truth by their own inductive rules. NeSyCat, extending ULLER, subsumes them under a single inductive definition of truth, parametric in a strong monad and an aggregation structure on truth-values. NeSyCat has so far lacked an account of predicates and functions learned by neural networks.
  We provide NeSyCat Torch as the missing link and interpret computational symbols via neural networks, implementing the framework in probabilistic programming and tensor-based backends. We use the distribution monad for reference semantics and metric evaluation, and complement it by a monad for numerically stable, differentiable training: the lazy log-tensor monad over the log-semiring. For efficient training in batches, we furthermore employ a batch monad. The axioms are the source code: written once in monad-based do-notation, monadic bind performs marginalisation, lazily pruning unneeded branches.
  On MNIST addition, our HaskTorch, JAX, and PyTorch implementations outperform LTN and DeepProbLog in speed and accuracy, while achieving nearly the accuracy of DeepStochLog. However, unlike DeepStochLog, we stay in a uniform framework that applies to many first-order NeSy approaches. Namely, the construction is parametric in the monad; instantiating it with, e.g., the Giry monad extends the approach to continuous probability (working out a neural representation here is left for future work).

</details>


### [316] [Rethinking Reward Supervision: Rubric-Conditioned Self-Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19327)
*Siyi Gu,Jialin Chen,Sophia Zhou,Arman Cohan,Rex Ying*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出Rubric-Conditioned Self-Distillation框架，利用结构化评分标准（rubrics）生成细粒度token级反馈，替代传统标量奖励或单一参考推理链，在科学推理任务上平均超越GRPO 1.0分、OPSD 0.9分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有后训练方法存在两类问题：(1) 监督蒸馏依赖昂贵且可能含噪声的思维链标注；(2) 基于验证奖励的强化学习将反馈压缩为标量信号，无法指明具体改进方向。两者均缺乏细粒度、结构化的过程级反馈。

Method: 提出Rubric-Conditioned Self-Distillation框架，两阶段流水线：(1) 学习生成任务特定rubrics；(2) 训练rubric引导的推理器。通过教师模型基于rubrics对学生自身采样的轨迹提供token级指导，实现细粒度信用分配。

Result: 在多种科学推理基准上，rubric条件自蒸馏平均超越GRPO 1.0分、OPSD 0.9分，有效将rubric级标准转化为token级推理过程指导。

Conclusion: Rubric条件自蒸馏通过结构化、细粒度的rubric反馈替代标量奖励或单一推理链，显著提升推理语言模型的后训练效果，为缺乏高质量标注的场景提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Post-training of reasoning language models is commonly driven by supervised distillation and reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards. Distillation often relies on chain-of-thought annotations that are expensive to obtain and may themselves be noisy, incomplete, or partially incorrect; even when the final solution is correct, an imperfect rationale can interfere with learning. Reinforcement learning with verified rewards, on the other hand, typically compresses evaluative feedback into a scalar signal, obscuring which aspects of a response should be improved. We propose \textbf{Rubric-Conditioned Self-Distillation}, a framework that incorporates rubrics as structured, fine-grained feedback for on-policy self-distillation. Our method conditions the teacher model on criterion-level rubrics and uses it to provide token-level guidance on the student's own sampled trajectories. This design avoids treating a single reference rationale as the sole supervision target. Instead, rubrics specify what a strong response should satisfy, enabling more fine-grained credit assignment over the reasoning process than scalar reward optimization. We instantiate this framework with a two-stage pipeline that first learns to generate task-specific rubrics and then trains a rubric-guided reasoner. We evaluate on a diverse suite of science reasoning benchmarks and results show that rubric-conditioned self-distillation effectively converts rubric-level criteria into token-level guidance over the reasoning process, surpassing GRPO by 1.0 points and OPSD by 0.9 points on average.

</details>
